 Dr
 Cardiac Sciences and Head Cardio Vascular Surgeon of Manipal Hospitals, Dwarka, New Delhi

 Today this percentage has reduced to 15 respectively
 4 fisadi or 10 fisadi rah gaya he
 Tax exemption is also a subsidy
 2006-07 ke baad se hi kendriya bajet main is baat kaa zikr hota he ki kitna rajasav ganvaaya gaya he
 The bottom line is that tax / GDP ratio is 5 if there is no exemption
 5 fisadi zyada hota
 Economics is an account of the use of resources
 har sansaadhan kaa koi or istemaal ho saktaa he
 Subsidies are difficult to calculate because not all subsidies are clearly visible
 thode se puraane ho gaye aankadon ko dekhen to sabsidi sakal gharelu utpaada kaa 14 pratishat he
 This is money that could have been spent elsewhere

" ye hai meri praathamiktaayen

 ''sabsidi ko vargeekrut karne ke alag-alag tareeke hote hai- lokhit main di jane vaali sabsidi, aavashyaktaanusaar sabsidi (jisase sakaaratmak antar najar aae) or iske baad gairajaruri sabsidi (gaiyr-praathamikta)

 jaruri sabsidi ke udhaaharan praathmik swasthya, saarvajanik swasthya, swatchta, sivej niptaan, sadak or pulon ko sabsidi muhaiyaa karana he

 isliye unase bachaa janaa chahie

 koi garib ko sabsidi dena chahta he

 isse pehle, mumbai ne landal simons (65) or kirone pollard (41) kii shandaar pariyon kii badaulat nirdhaarit 20 overon main chah wicket khokar 187 ranon kaa chunauteepurn score khadaa kiya
 Captain Rohit Sharma won the toss and decided to bat and both of his openers Simmons and Parthiv Patel (35) gave the team a brilliant start, citing their captain's fearless playing statement
 simons ne patel ke saath pehle wicket ke liye 10

 Bravo catches Patel at the hands of Ravindra Jadeja and finally gives Super Kings the first success
 patel ne 25 gendon main chaar chauke or ek chakka lagaaya
 After that, with the captain Rohit (19), who came out to bat, he could add 23 runs for the second wicket that Jadeja caught Simmons at the hands of Pawan Negi and defended the growing threat on the Super Kings
 simons ne is bich 51 gendon kii apni ardhashtakeey pari main teen chauke or paanch chakke lagaae
 This is Simmons' fifth half-century in IPL-8, making him the joint batsman for Mumbai Indians with Sachin Tendulkar and JP Duminy for the most fifties in any one edition
 15 overon main do wicket par 135 ran bana chuki mumbai ke liye haalanki agle do over kaaphi kharaab rahe
 In these two overs, Mumbai lost the wickets of Rohit and Hardik Pandya (1) in adding six runs
 rohit kaa wicket braavo ne jabaki pandya kaa wicket ashish nehra ne liya
 Pollard, who was present at the crease, though showing a sharp hand, hit a four and a six in 17 balls to give the team a challenging score
 is bich ambati rayudu (10) mohit sharma kaa shikaar hue
 The comments pollard bhi aakhri over kii chauthi gend par braavo kii gend ko kaaphi ooncha khel baithe or suresh raina ne kaich lene main koi galati nahin kii
 Bravo grabbed the highest three wickets for Chennai and with this, his total wickets in the IPL-8 has gone up to 23 and he remains the highest wicket-taker in the IPL-8
 iske baad ballebaaji karne aae phalf du plasis (45) ne maaikel hasi (16) ke saath duusare wicket ke liye 46 or suresh raina (25) ke saath tisare wicket ke liye 40 ranon kii saajhedaari kar team kii ummid banaae rakhi
 Hussey meanwhile was caught behind the wicket on the first ball of the sixth over brought by Vinay Kumar
 raina, plasis kii jodi sadhane kii koshishon main hi lagi hui thi ki 11waan over lekar aae mumbai indiens ke anbhavi spin gendbaaj harbhajan singh ne lagaataar do gendon par raina or captain mahendra singh dhoni (0) ke wicket chatka kar super kings kii ummiido par bijli gira di
 Plessis, however, did not give up hope and added 24 runs for the fifth wicket with Dwayne Bravo (20)
 ran gati badhaane kii koshishon main lage plasis ne jagadisha suchit kii gend ko leg said main ooncha khelaa haalanki long on par khadey vinay kumaar ne yah kaich aasaani se le liya
 Plessis faced 34 balls with five fours and a six
 plasis ke jate hi super kings kii museebataan bhi shuru ho gayi or agle do overon main braavo or pawan negi (3) bhi pavilion laut gaye

 negi, vinay kumaar kii gend par sthanapann kshetrarakshak unmukt chand ke haathon lapke gaye

 haalanki sari koshishon ke baavjood super kings kii puri team ek over pehle hi 162 ranon par pavilion laut gai
